Milan Kumar Hazra | Chemistry | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Faculty by Research Area Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Post Graduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Events Webinar Series ChemMeet 2024 Seminar Laboratories Teaching Laboratories Facilities About Facilities Booking for Internal Sample Booking for External Sample Contact Chemistry Milan Kumar Hazra Milan Kumar Hazra Assistant Professor school Ph.D: Indian Institute of Science email milanhazra[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Theoretical Physical Chemistry and Computational Biophysics call 0291 280 1308 language Web Profile Biography Milan obtained his bachelor’s degree in chemistry from Calcutta University in 2011 and joined the Integrated PhD program in chemical Science division at Indian Institute of Science (IISc), Bangalore. He pursued his doctoral research and received his PhD in theoretical physical chemistry under the supervision of Professor Biman Bagchi in 2019 from Solid State and Structural Chemistry Unit, IISc. During his doctoral research, Milan thoroughly investigated the phenomena of collective relaxations and it’s connection to solvation dynamics in dipolar binary mixtures and even went on to decode liquid state structure-dynamics paradigm of proteins and small molecules in aqueous media with the aids of computational battery and understandings borrowed from fundamental statistical mechanics. Thereafter in 2019, for his postdoctoral studies, Milan moved to the Department of Chemical and Structural Biology at Weizmann Institute of Science, Israel and was mentored by Professor Yaakov Levy. During his stay, he was primarily interested in decoding the molecular Grammer of phase separation in disordered proteins and thermodynamic origin of their ultra-high affinity. Currently he is serving as an assistant professor in the department of chemistry, IIT Jodhpur. In his free times, Milan loves reading Sci-Fi and thrillers, photography and outdoor games. Current Research We are a budding group of theoretical physical chemists and computational biophysicists fascinated to understand minute rhythm in biological systems in diverse time and length scales. Blending molecular simulations with the formulations of statistical mechanics, we are currently aiming toward developing (I) An understanding of entropy mediated subtle molecular recognition processes. (II) A consensus of thermodynamic and kinetic roles of IDR conformational ensembles in dynamic autoinhibition. (III) A molecular picture elucidating the role functional disorder in molecular chaperones. (IV) In addition, with our mesoscale structure-based coarse-grained simulation approach, we are actively looking at chromatin organization in cell nucleus at molecular length scales. (V) Apart from finding the answers of fundamental problems at the interface of chemistry and biology, we even develop and employ new computational methods to study problems of our interest. Jitendra Kumar | Physics | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Research Publication Research Groups Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Laboratories Contact Physics Jitendra Kumar Jitendra Kumar Assistant Professor school PhD: Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur email jitendrak[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Thin-Film Photovoltaic Devices, Nanomaterials, Semiconductor Devices, Micro-fabrication Technologies, Materials for Energy Applications, and Flexible Electronic Devices. call 0291 280 1609 language Web Profile Biography Dr. Jitendra Kumar is Joint Faculty in the Department of Physics and the Department of Metallurgical & Materials Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur. He completed his B.Tech. in Electronics & Communication Engineering from Uttar Pradesh Technical University, Lucknow, in 2009, followed by an M.Tech. in Nanotechnology from the Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee in 2011. Dr. Kumar earned his Ph.D. from the Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur in 2019, where his research focused on the synthesis and characterization of solution-processed Cu2ZnSnS4 thin films for solar cell applications. After completing his Ph.D., Dr. Kumar worked as an Institute Postdoctoral Fellow at the Indian Institute of Technology Delhi until 2020. During this tenure, his research primarily focused on the synthesis of inorganic perovskite nanocubes (CsPbIxBr3-x) using a hot-injection technique for solar cell applications. From 2020 to 2023, he held a postdoctoral position at Ben-Gurion University of the Negev, Israel, where his research centered on (BixSb1-x)2Se3-based solar cells. Between August 2023 and April 2025, he served as an INSPIRE Faculty at IIT Dhanbad, leading research on BaZrS3 thin-film solar cells. In February and March 2025, he was Marie Curie Fellow at INL – International Iberian Nanotechnology Laboratory. Dr. Kumar has received several prestigious honors, including the Marie Sklodowska-Curie Award in 2024 and the Marie Sklodowska-Curie Seal of Excellence in 2023. He was also awarded the INSPIRE Faculty Fellowship in 2023. Additionally he received international travel grants from EPFL and DST, which enabled him to present his research in Switzerland in 2021 and in the USA in 2018. He won the Best Poster Presentation Award at the IEEE Conference in Bangalore in 2018. Dr. Kumar has actively participated in and presented his work at numerous international conferences. Furthermore, he has been a visiting researcher at Martin Luther University, Halle-Wittenberg, Germany, in 2015 and at the Centre for Nanoscience & Engineering at the Indian Institute of Science Bangalore in 2014. Research Our research group is dedicated to the exploring advanced materials for energy applications, with a special emphasis on the development of inorganic thin-film solar cells. We strive to contribute to a sustainable future by advancing the innovation in materials design, fabrication and device engineering. Feel free to explore our work, meet our team, and join us in building a cleaner and greener future. Subrata Chakraborty | Chemistry | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! He pursued his doctoral studies at the University of Zurich, Switzerland and received the degree in 2013. He joined the group of Prof. David Milstein at Weizmann Institute of Science, Israel as a SFWIS Postdoctoral Fellow in 2014 and explored the research area of Organometallics and Homogeneous Catalysis with particular focus on Sustainability. Then he moved to University of Muenster, Germany in the group of Prof. Gerhard Erker as an AvH Fellow in 2018. After a brief stint at Muenster, he joined the Department of Chemistry, IIT Jodhpur as an Assistant Professor in June 2019. Research Our group is interested in studying Organometallic Catalysis, which shape and guide the chemical processes of the Industry. Our research work focuses on designing organometallic complexes bearing pincer and non-pincer nitrogen, phosphine and carbene based ligands. We explore the designed novel systems in homogeneous catalytic reactions, which play a pivotal role in the synthesis of industrially important molecules for fine chemicals, pharmaceuticals, agrochemical and so on. She earned her Ph.D. and M.Sc. in Mathematics from IIT Kharagpur, following a B.Sc. (Hons.) in Mathematics from Bankura Christian College. Her research specializes in Numerical Functional Analysis, particularly in approximation methods for integral and integro-differential equations, fixed point theory, and operator theory. With teaching experience spanning IIT Jodhpur and VIT University, she has offered a wide range of undergraduate and postgraduate courses, including Numerical Analysis, Functional Analysis, and Scientific Computations. She has authored over 15 journal articles in reputed international journals and contributed to several conferences and workshops. Dr. Mandal has been recognized with prestigious fellowships and grants, including a Postdoctoral Fellowship from NBHM and multiple research grants from NBHM and IIT Jodhpur. She serves as a reviewer for Mathematical Reviews and holds memberships in several mathematical societies such as AMS, RMS, and IMS. She is also on the editorial board of journals in mathematics and computational sciences. Her supervision includes guiding multiple master’s and doctoral students, with active research projects funded by Indian government agencies. Shyam Kumar Banjare | Chemistry | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Faculty by Research Area Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Post Graduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Events Webinar Series ChemMeet 2024 Seminar Laboratories Teaching Laboratories Facilities About Facilities Booking for Internal Sample Booking for External Sample Contact Chemistry Shyam Kumar Banjare Shyam Kumar Banjare Assistant Professor school Ph.D.: National Institute of Science Education and Research (NISER), Bhubaneswar email shyambanjare[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Research Interests in Transition Metal Catalysis, N-Heterocyclic Carbene Chemistry, and Organic Synthesis call 0291 280 1319 language Web Profile Biography Shyam Kumar Banjare earned his Bachelor of Science degree from Government M.M.R.P.G. College, Champa, and his Master of Science degree in Chemistry from Government Autonomous Science College Bilaspur, both affiliated with Bilaspur University, in 2013 and 2015, respectively. After completing his master’s degree, he qualified for the CSIR–NET–LS. He subsequently served as a temporary faculty member in the Department of Chemistry at Guru Ghasidas Vishwavidyalaya (a Central University), Bilaspur, from 2016 to 2017. He later joined the National Institute of Science Education and Research (NISER), Bhubaneswar, as a Junior Research Fellow under the supervision of Prof. Ponneri C. Ravikumar, where he completed his doctoral degree in March 2023. His PhD research focused on cobalt-catalyzed C–H bond functionalization. Following his doctoral studies, he joined the University of Münster, Germany, as a postdoctoral researcher with Prof. Armido Studer, where his research centered on radical reactions and photoredox chemistry. He is currently serving as an Assistant Professor at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur, with research interests in transition metal catalysis, N-heterocyclic carbene chemistry and organic synthesis. Academic Award Recipient of the Outstanding Doctoral Student Award (Best Thesis) from the Homi Bhabha National Institute HBNI, Mumbai, India, in 2024. Research His research program focuses on the design and development of innovative and broadly applicable catalytic platforms for contemporary organic synthesis. We harness the unique reactivity of N-heterocyclic carbenes (NHCs), both as privileged ligands in transition-metal catalysis and as powerful organocatalysts, to enable challenging C–C, C–N, and C–X bond-forming and bond-activation processes. By synergistically integrating transition-metal catalysis with NHC catalysis and Lewis acid activation, our approach enables precise molecular construction, exceptional efficiency, and high levels of chemo-, regio-, and stereoselectivity, while uncovering fundamentally new reaction manifolds. This research program offers an intellectually stimulating environment for students to engage in state-of-the-art catalysis, gain deep mechanistic understanding, and make creative, impactful contributions toward advancing the frontiers of catalytic science and synthetic methodology. Research Objectives: Develop innovative NHC-based catalytic systems for modern organic synthesis. Integrate transition-metal catalysis with NHCs to achieve synergistic reactivity Train students in state-of-the-art catalytic methods and mechanistic analysis. Discover new reaction manifolds and gain fundamental mechanistic insights in catalysis. Indian Institute of Technology Gandhinagar email saran[dot]aadhar[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Surface Hydrology; Hydroclimatic extremes; Hydrologic modeling in natural and anthropogenic climate; Impact of climate variability and climate change on water resources call 0291 280 1662 language Web Profile About: Dr. Saran Aadhar is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Civil and Infrastructure Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur and is affiliated with the Center for Intelligent Infrastructure, School of AI and Data Sciences . His research focuses on real-time monitoring of drought and floods, sub-seasonal to seasonal forecasting of hydrological extremes, hydrological processes under changing and anthropogenic climates, and the impact of climate change on water resources . Dr. Aadhar earned his Ph.D. in Civil Engineering from the Indian Institute of Technology Gandhinagar in 2021 and completed his B.Tech. in Civil Engineering from the National Institute of Technology Raipur in 2015. As part of his academic journey, he was a Visiting Scholar at the University of Nebraska-Lincoln, USA in 2019. Before joining IIT Jodhpur, he worked as a Postdoctoral Researcher at the Hebrew University of Jerusalem, Israel , from December 2020 to November 2021. Recognized for his contributions to hydrology and climate science, Dr. Aadhar has received numerous prestigious awards and honors. He is a Young Associate of the Indian Academy of Sciences and a recipient of the 2024 CDRI Fellowship . His research excellence has been acknowledged with the Best Discussion Award (2022) by the Journal of Hydrological Engineering (ASCE) and the Sivapalan Young Scientists Travel Award from the International Association of Hydrological Sciences (IAHS) . Additionally, he has been awarded the Water Advanced Research and Innovation (WARI) Fellowship by the Indo-U.S. Science and Technology Forum , the Ministry of Education Ph.D. Fellowship (2015-2020), and travel grants from SERB, SPARC, and ITRA . He has also received the IIT Gandhinagar Cash Research Award for his outstanding academic contributions. With a strong foundation in hydrological modeling and climate impact assessment, Dr. Aadhar continues to contribute to cutting-edge research aimed at improving water resource management and mitigating the risks of extreme hydrological events. Arun Kumar R | Mechanical Engineering | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctorial Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Laboratories Contact Mechanical Engineering Arun Kumar R Arun Kumar R Associate Professor school PhD. Indian Institute of Technology Madras email arunkr[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Experimental Aerodynamics - Confined Jets, Shock Wave Reflection and Transitions, Ejector Flows. call 0291 280 1516 About Arun Kumar R is an Associate Professor in the Department of Mechanical Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur . His area of expertise lies in high-speed flows and shock waves . He has established the Shock Waves and High-Speed Flow Laboratory (SWAHS Lab) at IIT Jodhpur, which focuses on experimental and computational research related to supersonic and hypersonic flow phenomena, including fuel injection, mixing enhancement, and blast wave interactions. The Shock Waves and High-Speed Flow Laboratory (SWAHS Lab) is dedicated to advancing the frontiers of research and technology development in the aerospace and defense sectors . In addition to traditional high-speed aerodynamic applications, the lab actively explores multidisciplinary extensions of shock wave and high-speed flow research into fields such as refrigeration systems, biomedical engineering, industrial processing, and water purification . Ongoing research includes projects on supersonic intakes , supersonic air-fuel mixing in scramjet combustors , flow control and actuators , gas turbine cooling , electric propulsion systems , shock and blast wave attenuation , as well as novel applications like solar ejector refrigeration , steam ejector-based water purification , and shock wave-assisted biomedical techniques . He works in the research areas of carbon capture, utilization, and storage (CCUS), waste valorization, and nanomaterials within the cement and concrete value chain. Dr. Sargam earned his Ph.D. (2021) and M.S. (2019) from Iowa State University, USA, under the supervision of Prof. Kejin Wang. His doctoral work on the dispersion and stability of nanomaterials in cementitious systems earned him the Research Excellence Award from the university. His master’s research was focused on the measurement and prediction of mass concrete parameters and thermal conductivity. After his graduate studies, Dr. Sargam worked at CarbonCure Technologies, Canada (2021–2025), where he held roles of Research Scientist, Director of Research, and Senior Director of Research. During his tenure, he played a key role in advancing the understanding of CO2 mineralization mechanisms and developing CO2 utilization technologies for low-carbon concrete. Dr. Sargam has published extensively in high-impact journals, including Cement and Concrete Research, Journal of CO₂ Utilization, and Composites Part B, and actively collaborates with renowned researchers worldwide. His detailed research profile is available on Google Scholar . If you are interested in joining Dr. Sargam’s research group or would like to collaborate with him, please reach out to him at ysargam@iitj.ac.in . Swati Jindal | Chemistry | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Faculty by Research Area Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Post Graduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Events Webinar Series ChemMeet 2024 Seminar Laboratories Teaching Laboratories Facilities About Facilities Booking for Internal Sample Booking for External Sample Contact Chemistry Swati Jindal Swati Jindal Assistant Professor school Ph.D: Indian Institute of Technology , Kanpur email sjindal[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Synthetic Materials Chemistry/Hybrid Porous Frameworks (MOFs/COFs) call 0291 280 1317 language Web Profile Biography Dr. Swati Jindal obtained her Master’s degree in Chemistry from the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Hyderabad in 2016. She pursued her doctoral studies at the IIT Kanpur under the supervision of Prof. J. N. Moorthy, receiving her Ph.D. in 2022. During her doctoral research, she focused on the design and synthesis of luminescent metal–organic frameworks (MOFs) for analyte sensing applications. Following her Ph.D., she joined the research group of Prof. Mohamed Eddaoudi at the King Abdullah University of Science and Technology (KAUST), Saudi Arabia, as a Postdoctoral Fellow in 2022, where she broadened her research scope to include the development of covalent organic frameworks (COFs) and their applications in sensing, energy storage, and optical devices. In September 2025, Dr. Jindal joined the Department of Chemistry, Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur, as an Assistant Professor. Research Our research group focuses on the rational design and synthesis of organic building blocks to construct functionalized porous materials, including metal–organic frameworks (MOFs) and covalent organic frameworks (COFs). These crystalline materials offer highly ordered pores, tunable functionality, accessible surface active sites, and large surface areas, making them promising candidates for diverse advanced applications. We are particularly interested in developing hybrid porous functionalized frameworks (HPFFs) that integrate the advantages of both organic and inorganic components. Through controlled molecular engineering and structure–property correlation studies, our research aims to explore these materials for environmental remediation, photocatalytic hydrogen evolution, energy storage, and optical applications. A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Technical Staff Members Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Project Staff Members Research Publication Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Research Overview Academic Programs Regulations Undergraduate Program Postgraduate program Doctoral Program Curriculum Laboratories Calender Contact Electrical Engineering Vineeth V Vineeth V Assistant Professor school Ph. D.: Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur email vineeth[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Power Systems, Active Distribution System Operational Planning, Smart Grids, Distributed Energy Resources, Optimization call 0291 280 1399 About Dr. Vineeth Vijayan is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Electrical Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur and a Faculty Affiliate at the Rishabh Centre for Innovation and Research in Clean Energy. He obtained his Ph.D. from IIT Kanpur (2023), M.Tech. from the University of Kerala, Thiruvananthapuram (2013), and B.E. from Anna University, Chennai (2010). From November 2023 to April 2025, he was a Postdoctoral Researcher at the Center for Energy Systems Research, Tennessee Tech University, USA. His research focuses on the operational planning of active electric distribution networks, including renewable energy integration, demand-side management, Volt/VAR control, and topology optimization. His emerging interests include grid-scale energy storage systems, e-mobility, cyber-resilience, and quantum applications in power systems. Dr. Vijayan has received several notable recognitions, including the Dr. Shankar Dayal Sharma Medal for best all-round post-graduating student of IIT Kanpur, the Trilok Chandra Goel Memorial Gold Medal for research contributing to sustainable energy, and the IIT Kanpur Excellence Award for leadership in student affairs (all in 2023). He was also awarded the IIT Kanpur Gymkhana Blues (2022), the DST AWSAR Award (2021), and the IEEE India Council Outstanding Volunteer Award (2020). He has published research in reputed venues, including IEEE Transactions and leading international conferences. An active IEEE volunteer, he has served as Secretary of the IEEE Power & Energy Society (Asia-Pacific Region, Region 10) and as Chair of the Educational and Technical Activities Subcommittee of the IEEE PES Global Student Chapters Committee. Pankaj Yadav | Bioscience & Bioengineering | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment About Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctorial Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Laboratories Contact Bioscience & Bioengineering Pankaj Yadav Pankaj Yadav Associate Professor school PhD. Christian Albrechts Universität zu Kiel Germany email pyadav[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Statistical Genetics, Deep Learning, Big Data Analytics call 0291 280 1211 language Web Profile About Education: Dr. Yadav obtained his first academic degree in 2009 as Bachelor of Engineering in Biotechnology from Panjab University, Chandigarh, India. He then moved to Germany, where he spent nearly eight years pursuing advanced studies. In 2012, he completed his Master of Science in Life Science Informatics from the University of Bonn, Germany. Following this, he obtained his Doctoral Degree in Statistical Genomics from the University of Kiel, Germany, in 2015, with funding from the German Research Foundation (DFG). Professional career: Since December 2024, Dr. Yadav has been working as an Associate Professor in the Bioscience & Bioengineering Department at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT), Jodhpur. Prior to this, from June 2019 to December 2024, he served as an Assistant Professor at IIT Jodhpur. He is also an affiliated faculty member at the School of Artificial Intelligence & Data Science at IIT Jodhpur. Before joining IIT Jodhpur, Dr. Yadav worked as a Senior Data Scientist at Reliance Jio, Hyderabad, India, and as a Research Scientist at DuPont, Hyderabad, India. From November 2016 to July 2018, he worked as a Postdoctoral Scientist at the renowned German Cancer Research Center (DKFZ) in Heidelberg, Germany. Additionally, in 2012, he served as a Research Assistant at the Helmholtz Research Center, Munich, Germany. Research work: Dr. Yadav's primary research interests include statistical genetics, personalized healthcare, multi-omics, and the application of deep learning in multi-omics data analysis. With over 10 years of experience in genome-wide gene-environment interaction studies, method development, and integrated multi-omics data analysis, he has made significant contributions to these fields. He is currently serving as the Principal Investigator (PI) for the Genome India project, funded by the Department of Biotechnology (DBT), Government of India, where he has been actively involved in various aspects of the analysis of Indian genomes, with a particular focus on gene-environment interactions. Additionally, he is leading an ICMR Intermediate Project aimed at identifying gene-environment and polygenic risk score-environment interactions in the Indian population to improve risk stratification for prediabetes and type 2 diabetes mellitus. Dr. Yadav has extensive experience in developing statistical methods for gene-environment interaction studies. During his time at DKFZ, he worked on drawing statistical inferences from multiple myeloma cancer datasets collected from hospitals in Germany and the UK. At the Helmholtz Center, Munich, he contributed to the development of machine learning algorithms for quantitative structure-activity relationship (QSAR) analysis. His research has been published in several peer-reviewed international journals, and he has contributed to numerous international conferences, seminars, and workshops. Dr. Yadav also serves as an invited review editor for the International Journal of Diabetes in Developing Countries and Frontiers in Genetics. Awards & honours: Dr. Yadav has received several prestigious awards and fellowships throughout his career. He was awarded an undergraduate scholarship from Panjab University to pursue his Bachelor of Engineering degree. He was also granted the German Research Foundation (DFG) Fellowship to complete his doctoral studies and later received the Deutsche Krebshilfe Postdoctoral Fellowship. In 2018, Dr. Yadav was honored with the INSPIRE Faculty Award by the Indian National Science Academy (INSA). The following year, in 2019, he received the “Returning Expert” Award from the German Development Cooperation (GIZ). In 2023, he was awarded a Travel Award by the Human Cell Atlas (HCA) to present his research at the HCA Asia meeting. That same year, his project was selected for the Scientific High-Level Visiting Fellowship (SSHN) by the French Institute in India, Embassy of France. Outside of his academic achievements, Dr. Yadav is also passionate about sports. In 2023, he earned a Gold Medal in Volleyball as the team captain at the Inter-IIT Staff Sports Meet held at IIT Gandhinagar. In 2025, Dr. Yadav was selected as a Senior Individual Member of the Indian National Academy of Engineering (INAE). Yogeshwar Nath Mishra | Physics | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Research Publication Research Groups Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Laboratories Contact Physics Yogeshwar Nath Mishra Yogeshwar Nath Mishra Assistant Professor school PhD: Lund University, Sweden email mishrayn[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Ultrafast Imaging, Laser Diagnostics, Photonics, Energy Technology, Biomedical Imaging call 0291 280 1624 Biography Dr. Yogeshwar Nath Mishra is an Assistant Professor at IIT Jodhpur. He earned his Ph.D. in Optics and Engineering Physics from Lund University, Sweden, in 2018, under the supervision of Prof. Edouard Berrocal, where he developed advanced laser diagnostics for probing optically dense media. He subsequently held postdoctoral and research scientist positions at FAU Erlangen in Germany, and jointly at the University of Gothenburg in Sweden and NASA’s Jet Propulsion Laboratory at the California Institute of Technology (Caltech) in the USA. He has been mentored by several globally renowned scientists and pioneers in their fields, including Prof. Lihong Wang (Caltech), Dr. Murthy Gudipati (NASA), and Prof. Wolfgang Heidrich (KAUST). Dr. Mishra has received numerous accolades, including the Indian Academy of Sciences Summer Research Fellowship (2010), Visiting Student Fellowship from Raman Research Institute (2011), SPIE Student Author Travel Award (2012), PETRA Awards for Young Researchers - ILASS Europe (2013), ÅForsk Foundation Scholarship (2015), Invited Speaker, Gordon Research Conference (2017), Swedish Research Council International Postdoctoral Fellowship (2018), Adlerbert Foundation Sustainable Research Fellowship – Gothenburg (2022), Dr. K. Radhakrishnan Young Scientist Award (2023) from ISEES–IIT Kanpur, and the Young Researcher Award (2025, Runner-up) from Erlangen Graduate School in Advanced Optical Technologies, FAU Erlangen, Germany. While at Caltech, he co-invented laser sheet compressed ultrafast photography (LS-CUP), a groundbreaking technique recognized as the World’s Fastest single-shot planar imaging method. This work, conducted under Prof. Lihong Wang, was among the top-downloaded articles in the prestigious Light: Science and Applications journal in 2023. More recently, he reported CUP2AI, recognized as the world’s fastest single-shot wide-field molecular mapping technique. His research has been featured in Physics World, Phys.org, EurekaAlert! (AAAS), Nature India, Swedish National Radio, Caltech, The Hindu, The Indian Express, The Lallantop, Republic TV, among other national and international news outlets. Dr. Mishra has served as an Adjunct Faculty at IIT Indore, where he founded Fourier Energy Solutions Pvt. Ltd. along with his colleagues, focusing on developing smart optical solutions for energy technology and biomedical research. Research We are young and dynamic team engaged in cutting-edge research in Optics and Photonics. Our group thrives on curiosity, creativity, and collaboration as we explore both fundamental science and real-world applications of optical technologies for a sustainable future and the benefit of society. Our research includes: Laser Diagnostics in engines, fuel cells, and photovoltaic systems. Ultrafast Science , focusing on light-matter interaction dynamics. Space Science , including adaptive optics and thermal/hyperspectral imaging. Quantum Technologies , with a focus quantum-enhanced imaging techniques. Biomedical Imaging and Artificial Intelligence: lab-on-chip diagnostic platforms for biomedial applications. We actively welcome enthusiastic students and researchers to join us. For internships, Ph.D. admissions, or self-sponsored positions, please contact with your CV. This project, titled "Socio-Economic Influences on the Intergenerational Transmission of Indigenous Occupational Skills in Western Rajasthan," investigates how traditional skills are passed down through generations and the socio-economic factors affecting this process. The study aims to provide valuable insights into cultural sustainability and socio-economic mobility in the region . Dr. Choudhary's research focuses on development economics, education and health economics, public policy, and gender studies, with a particular emphasis on intergenerational mobility. Her work contributes to understanding the dynamics of cultural heritage preservation and the socio-economic development of communities in Rajasthan. Sucharita Dey | Bioscience & Bioengineering | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment About Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctorial Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Laboratories Contact Bioscience & Bioengineering Sucharita Dey Sucharita Dey Assistant Professor school PhD. Bose Institute Kolkata email sdey[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Principles of protein robustness to mutation, Functional role of protein quaternary structure in mutation and disease, Prediction of disease mutations, Identifying structural determinants of inter-subunit communication -- Allostery call 0291 280 1218 language Web Profile Sucharita Dey Dr. Sucharita Dey is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Bioscience and Bioengineering at IIT Jodhpur. She completed her PhD in Computational Structural Biology from Bose Institute, Kolkata, in 2013, and postdoctoral training from Cancer Science Institute Singapore and Weizmann Institute of Science, Israel, from 2013 to 2021. She is a recipient of the Ramalingaswami fellowship and research grant 2021 from DBT India. She works in structural bioinformatics, where her research group broadly focuses on understanding the mechanisms underlying protein-protein interactions in the living cell. Her research group focuses explicitly on studying genetic variations among diverse populations and, hence, the mutational robustness of proteins. The aim is to understand disease mechanisms in the context of protein structure (specifically protein quaternary structure) variation. Her research interests also include studying the diversity and unveiling novel principles of protein-protein interactions, protein oligomerization and evolution, protein Quaternary structure prediction, identifying structural determinants of inter-subunit communication (Allostery), and designing molecules that act through an allosteric transition. Her group uses diverse computational methods to do structural analysis of bulk data. This ‘big data’ analysis on structural biology is anticipated to create a new field of ‘structuromics’ (bridging proteomics and interactomics with structural data), and her group at IIT Jodhpur would be actively contributing to it. Email: sdey@iitj.ac.in. His research interests include parameter optimization, aquifer scale modeling, dynamic plant uptake, source identification and application of one health. . Academic Contributions: Throughout his academic career, Dr. Swami has been actively involved in research and consultancy projects, contributing to the advancement of knowledge in his field. His expertise has been instrumental in shaping the curriculum and research initiatives at both IIT Mandi and IIT Jodhpur. ​ Professional Engagements: Dr. Swami has organized and participated in various workshops and conferences. Notably, he was involved in the HYDRUS Winter School held from January 27-31, 2024, aimed at educating participants on the use of HYDRUS software for research and consultancy purposes. Dr. Swami's transition to IIT Jodhpur marks a significant step in his career, where he continues to contribute to the field of civil and infrastructure engineering through his teaching, research, and professional activities. Research Dr. Dushyant Kumar's research investigates the fundamental properties and applications of novel quantum materials, with a significant emphasis on two-dimensional topological quantum materials. His work explores their intrinsic quantum properties, including nonlinearity, for applications in spintronics, energy harvesting, and sensing. His research group employs advanced device fabrication techniques, such as e-beam lithography, for the development of components relevant to quantum communication and quantum computing. The group's activities encompass thin film growth, device fabrication, and comprehensive electrical transport and optical measurements. His key research interests include Topological quantum materials for next-generation spintronic devices. Spin texture characterization in topological materials and perovskites. Nonlinear quantum properties for sensing and energy harvesting applications. Quantum rectification at high frequencies, spanning 4G, 5G, and up to THz. Device development for quantum communication and quantum computing technologies. Suresh Sarkar | Chemistry | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Faculty by Research Area Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Post Graduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Events Webinar Series ChemMeet 2024 Seminar Laboratories Teaching Laboratories Facilities About Facilities Booking for Internal Sample Booking for External Sample Contact Chemistry Suresh Sarkar Suresh Sarkar Assistant Professor school Ph.D.: Indian association for the cultivation of Science email sarkar[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Nanomaterials; NIR-Quantum dots; Spectroscopy; Surface Chemistry; Shape control; Photo-catalysis; photo-voltaics; cell-imaging call 0291 280 1346 language Web Profile Biography Suresh Sarkar is a dedicated researcher specializing in the synthesis and application of nanomaterials. He earned his PhD in 2014 from the Indian Association for the Cultivation of Science (IACS), Kolkata, under the mentorship of Professor Narayan Pradhan, where he made significant contributions to the field through extensive publications. Following his doctoral studies, he pursued postdoctoral research at Vanderbilt University, USA (2014–2016), further deepening his expertise in nanomaterials. He then undertook a second postdoctoral fellowship at the University of Illinois at Urbana-Champaign, USA, under Professor Andrew M. Smith, completing it in 2022. Currently, Dr. Sarkar serves as an Assistant Professor at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur. His research focuses on the development of advanced functional nanomaterials with applications in photovoltaics, catalysis, and related energy. His work aims to bridge the gap between fundamental nanoscience and real-world technological advancements, contributing to the next generation of high-performance materials. Research His research focuses on development of novel functional semiconductor nanomaterials and understand their crystal growth and photo-physical behaviour in solution. Surface engineering of quantum dots: Quantum dots are well-known for their quantum confinement and high surface to volume ratio. The surface structure/morphology of quantum dots plays pivotal role in controlling their photo-physical properties and applications in nanotechnology. Our research group focuses on surface engineering of quantum dots for achieving novel functional properties that can enhance their efficiency in nanotechnological applications. Transition Metal Ion Doping : Doping semiconductor nanocrystals with transition metal ions unlocks unique properties for optoelectronics. Our research explores optimal host-guest combinations to develop novel functional nanomaterials. Anisotropic Semiconductor Nanomaterials : They offer enhanced electron transport, making them ideal for optoelectronics, sensors, and photocatalysis. Our research focuses on designing tunable semiconductor nanocrystals for advanced catalytic applications. Heterostructure Nanomaterials: Integrating multiple components in a nanocrystal creates unique properties for applications in photovoltaics and photocatalysis. Our research focuses on synthesizing heterostructured nanomaterials and exploring their functional potential. Photovoltaics: Our research explores semiconductor nanomaterials for efficient solar energy conversion. We assess their light absorption potential and develop low-cost photodetectors to evaluate their suitability for next-generation solar cells. Photocatalysis: We develop near-infrared absorbing semiconductor nanocrystals for sustainable energy and organic synthesis. Our focus is on utilizing them in single-step reactions to produce commercially valuable compounds. He was also the first faculty-in-charge of IIT Jodhpur Technology Park during 2021-2023 and has mentored three start-ups. Further, he has served as Dean of Infrastructure Planning(DoIP) at IIT Jodhpur during Sept 2023 - Aug 2025. He has been honoured with several prestigious awards including the PSSI Jaidutt Saraswati Sodha Award (2022), SERC Fast Track Young Scientist Award (2003), BOYSCAST Fellowship (2005), and CSIR-CEERI’s Foundation Day Award for Excellence in Research (2018). He is one of the editors of Nature: Scientific Reports Journal, was a Vice-President of the Plasma Science Society of India during 2022–2024, and was also a scientific consultant to the International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA) in Vienna in the year 2009. His contributions to science communication in Hindi are well-known and he received a Vishesh Vaigyanik Rajbhasha Vishishtha Samman in the year 2012. Research Prof. Ram Prakash is currently working on low temperature plasma applications and spearheading the development of a state-of-the-art Cold Plasma Laboratory aimed at delivering innovative, plasma-based solutions in the fields of health, food, energy, and agriculture. His team has made significant research contributions using cold plasmas for clean air, water purity, environmental safety, and efficient energy systems. The unique aspects of his work are related to innovations that have involved design, development, and translation of fundamental research into devices and systems that can be used in the field by common man and industries. He has successfully developed six technologies -Four technologies for commercialization by industries and two technologies for strategic sectors. The work done on novel Cold-plasma Detergent in Environment (CODE) Device for better indoor air quality, Advanced Photocatalytic Oxidation Systems to fight COVID-19 pandemic, Mercury-Free-Plasma UV-lamps for efficient water disinfection, VUV-spectrometer-detector system calibration source useful for tokamak machines, Radial Multi-channel High-current Pseudospark Switch useful for high pulse power applications, Sheet-beam Plasma Cathode Electron Gun useful for THz microwave generation are a few of them to mention. Sudipta Bhattacharyya | Bioscience & Bioengineering | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment About Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctorial Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Laboratories Contact Bioscience & Bioengineering Sudipta Bhattacharyya Sudipta Bhattacharyya Associate Professor school PhD. Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur email sudipta[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Structural Biology, Enzyme Chemistry, Protein Engineering call 0291 280 1213 language Web Profile Sudipta Bhattacharyya Dr. Sudipta Bhattacharyya is an Associate professor in the Department of Bioscience and Bioengineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur. Dr. Bhattacharyya’s research is focused on unravelling the molecular intricacies of host-pathogen interactions and drug resistance. Dr. Bhattacharyya has completed his B.Sc in Microbiology (Honours) from Calcutta University, followed by an M.Sc in Microbiology and Microbial Technology from Kalyani University. He has earned Ph.D. in Biochemistry and Structural Biology from Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur. After completion of his PhD degree, Dr. Bhattacharyya completed his post-doctoral research tenures in Colorado State University, USA, University of Texas, USA and University of Melbourne, Australia. During his PhD and post-doctoral tenures, he has been extensively employed the state-of-the-art tools and techniques of Structural Biology, Enzyme Chemistry and Drug Designing. His postdoctoral research for the first time, excavated the ancestral origin of the modern nucleosome, which is the fundamental repeating unit of eukaryotic chromosomes. Moreover, his postdoctoral research works also shed light on the molecular basis of prokaryotic non-homologus end joining based dsDNA repair mechanism and the novel molecular conformation of HIV-I surface glycoprotein during cell entry and antibody dependent cellular cytotoxicity. At IIT Jodhpur, Dr. Bhattacharyya’s research group is principally engaged in structure-guided rational drug discovery against the dreaded ESKAPE pathogens, focusing on natural products and leveraging pharmacophore identification for the rational discovery of therapeutic leads. With a prolific academic career, Dr. Bhattacharyya has so far published more than 35 research papers in peer-reviewed international journals including the top tier journals in the field like Science, Cell Host & Microbe, PNAS etc., contributed more than 35 Protein Data Bank (PDB) and Electron Microscopy Data Bank (EMDB) -based publications, and applied for 4 Indian patents. His contributions to the scientific community extend beyond research as an active member of the American Chemical Society, the Royal Society of Biology, CCP4 Bulletin Board and Phenix Bulletin Board. He is committed to foster innovation in structure guided drug discovery by inspiring the next generation of researchers in the field. Indian Institute of Technology Delhi email skrishnan[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Material Characterization; Cement Chemistry; Concrete Technology; Durability and Repair of Structures; call 0291 280 1670 language Web Profile About: Dr. Sreejith Krishnan is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Civil and Infrastructure Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur . His research focuses on the chemistry of cementitious materials , with a particular interest in low-carbon cement development, hydration and microstructure of alternative binders, and sustainable construction materials . Before joining IIT Jodhpur, Dr. Krishnan was a Research Fellow at the University of Leeds, UK (2021–2023) , where he worked on the MUSE project under Prof. Susan Bernal , developing novel low-carbon cement from activated clays . Prior to that, he was a Postdoctoral Researcher at EPFL, Switzerland (2019–2020) , working with Prof. Karen Scrivener on the chemistry of belite in Portland cement through a Swiss Government Excellence Postdoctoral Fellowship . He obtained his Ph.D. in Civil Engineering from IIT Delhi (2019) under the supervision of Prof. Shashank Bishnoi , as part of the Low Carbon Cement Project , funded by the Swiss Agency for Development and Cooperation . His research focused on hydration and microstructure development in limestone calcined clay cements (LC3) and optimizing LC3 blend compositions . He also holds an M.Tech. in Construction Engineering and Management from IIT Delhi (2014) and a B.Tech. in Civil Engineering from NIT Calicut (2012) . Dr. Krishnan has been recognized for his contributions to cement chemistry and sustainable construction. He received the Distinction in Doctoral Research Award (IIT Delhi, 2019) , the Swiss Government Excellence Fellowship (2019) , the Advances in Cement Research Prize from the Institute of Civil Engineers, UK (2020) , and the Prime Minister’s Early Career Research Grant from ANRF, India (2025) . His expertise continues to drive advancements in sustainable construction materials and the development of alternative cementitious systems . A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Research Faculty by Research Area Publication About Research Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Post Graduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Events Webinar Series ChemMeet 2024 Seminar Laboratories Teaching Laboratories Facilities About Facilities Booking for Internal Sample Booking for External Sample Contact Chemistry Rahul Gera Rahul Gera Assistant Professor school Ph. D.: Tata Institute of Fundamental Research - Mumbai email rahulgera[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Spectroscopy, Molecular Self-assemblies, Photophysics and Photochemistry call 0291 280 1316 About Dr. Rahul Gera completed his Ph.D. at the Tata Institute of Fundamental Research in 2016. Following his doctoral studies, he pursued postdoctoral research at the University of Pennsylvania from 2016 to 2018. He then joined AMOLF in the Netherlands for subsequent postdoctoral work from 2019 to 2021, followed by a research fellow appointment at the Nanyang Technological University from 2022 to 2023. In 2024, Dr. Gera joined the Regional Institute of Education, a constituent unit of the National Council of Educational Research and Training (NCERT), as an Assistant Professor, where he served until 2025. In April 2025, Dr. Gera joined the Department of Chemistry at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur as an Assistant Professor Research Interest At the Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur, Dr. Rahul Gera aims to establish a research program focused on developing molecular self-assemblies for controlling photochemical reactivity at the nanoscale. Utilizing his experience in host–guest chemistry, supramolecular self-assemblies, and nonlinear optical spectroscopic methods, such as femtosecond transient absorption spectroscopy and vibrational sum-frequency generation spectroscopy, he aspires to develop novel strategies for driving selective photochemistry both in solution and at interfaces. His group designs and synthesizes self-assembled nanocages to encapsulate and stabilize reactive guest molecules, enabling access to unique light-driven reaction pathways under molecular confinement. They investigate ultrafast excited-state dynamics and key physical properties using state-of-the-art spectroscopy. The group aims to uncover how confined environments reshape photochemical behaviour. During her PhD at the Department of Cell and Molecular Physiology at the University of North Carolina at Chapel Hill, Prof Jha elucidated a novel pathway for inflammation and demyelination in the brain. She pursued Postdoctoral research at the UNC Lineberger Comprehensive Cancer Care (USA), characterising cellular and molecular mechanisms of demyelination in Multiple Sclerosis. Subsequently, Prof Jha joined IIT Jodhpur in 2012. At IIT Jodhpur, she established the Inflammation Immunity and Tumour Biology Lab. This lab focuses on understanding innate immunity, inflammation, and tumour biology utilising cellular and molecular 3-Dimensional (3D) models such as patient-derived organoids and 3D tunable spheroids to study brain tumours and breast cancer pathophysiology as well as normal physiology. Prof Jha's laboratory has been funded by the Department of Biotechnology, International Brain Research Organization (IBRO), Department of Science and Technology, Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology (MEITy), SERB, and BRNS (DAE). Prof Jha is the recipient of the IITJ Research Excellence Award 2024, IBRO Diversity grant 2023, ISNO President’s Award for Outstanding Work in Neuro-Oncology by the Indian Society for Neuro-Oncology (2022), The Kusum Sharma Award for a Young Woman Scientist awarded by the Indian Academy of Biomedical Sciences (2021), Young scientist Award, (2014-2017) Science and Engineering Research Board (SERB), and the Hulka Innovator’s Award (2008) Centre for women’s health research at University of North Carolina Chapel Hill, USA. Prof Jha is the founding Head of the Department of Bioscience and Bioengineering at IITJ and has been heading the joint programs in medical technologies between IITJ and AIIMSJ since 2020, as well as the MedTech Centre at IITJ. His research interests primarily are simulating turbulent flows and developing novel and green technologies, such as MILD combustion or hydrogen-based combustion. He is a skilled researcher on numerical simulations of reacting flows and its analysis using domain-specific and machine learning (ML) techniques. Prior to joining IIT-Jodhpur, he has worked for a year as a Lead Engineer – Combustion Modelling in GE Vernova, Bangalore. Between 2019 and 2023, he worked as an IF@ULB (Marie-Curie COFUND) postdoctoral fellow in ULB, Belgium, working on application of ML on combustion datasets. Between 2014 and 2019, he completed his PhD from the Indian Institute of Science (IISc) Bangalore in Aerospace Engineering working on direct numerical simulations (DNS) of turbulent premixed hydrogen-air flames. Between 2010 and 2014, he worked on liquid rocket engines as a Scientist/Engineer at Liquid Propulsions Systems Center (LPSC), ISRO. He holds a BE(Hons.) in Mechanical Engineering from BITS-Pilani, Goa Campus. His research focuses on studying and modeling climate change impacts on hydrological systems, statistical analysis of hydrological time series, and the application of wavelet transformation and copula theory in hydroclimatic analysis . He earned his Ph.D. from IIT Kharagpur (2020) , where his research, under the supervision of Prof. Rajib Maity , focused on the analysis and modeling of climate change impact on hydrological extreme events across India . He also holds an M.Tech. in Civil Engineering from IIT Kharagpur (2015) and a B.Tech. in Civil Engineering from NIT Hamirpur (2013) . Before joining IIT Jodhpur, Dr. Suman held research positions at leading institutions. He worked as a Postdoctoral Researcher at Pohang University of Science and Technology, South Korea (Sep 2021 – Feb 2022) in the Division of Environmental Science and Engineering . He also served as a Research Associate at IIT Kharagpur (Jan 2021 – July 2021) in the Department of Civil Engineering . Beyond academia, Dr. Suman is an open-source enthusiast and a contributor to multiple open-source projects , earning the title of Arctic Code Vault Contributor for GitHub's 2020 Code Archive Program . Additionally, he is a martial artist , holding a First-Degree Black Belt (Shodan) in Kyokushin-kan Karate . West Virginia University email richa[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Machine Learning; Pattern Recognition; Biometrics; Forensics; Trusted AI call 0291 280 1267 language Web Profile About ​D​r. Singh is a Professor in the Department of Computer Science and Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur. She earned her Ph.D. in Computer Science from West Virginia University, USA. She is a globally recognized leader in artificial intelligence and machine learning, with a focus on pattern recognition, biometrics, medical image analysis, and Responsible AI. Her contributions to the field have been recognized with the highest distinctions, including being named a Fellow of the IEEE, IAPR, and Indian National Academy of Engineering (INAE). She is also an ACM Distinguished Member and a member of the National Academy of AI (USA). A prolific researcher, Prof. Singh has authored over 400 publications in top-tier venues, which have garnered more than 16,200 citations (h index: 71). Her research program has attracted external grants exceeding Rs. 56 crores. She holds editorial leadership roles, serving as the Founding Co-Editor-in-Chief of ACM AI Letters and the Associate Editor-in-Chief of the prestigious Pattern Recognition Journal. Prof. Singh's work has demonstrated profound real-world impact. Her face recognition technology was instrumental in the challenging task of identifying victims of the Balasore train accident, while her deepfake detection systems were deployed to ​p​revent the​ spread of misinformation ​i​n India's 2024 general elections. Her contributions have been honored with numerous awards, including the Nasscom AI Gamechangers Award and the Facebook Award for Ethics in AI. She has supervised 14 Ph.D. students to graduation (14 ongoing PhDs) and guided over 200 M.Tech and B.Tech students. She has a strong record of service to the academic community, notably serving as the Program Committee Chair for CVPR 2022, becoming the first researcher from India to hold this position in the conference's 40-year history. She regularly serves in leadership roles for premier conferences such as ICCV, ECCV, AAAI, and major biometrics venues. Lata Panwar | Physics | IIT Jodhpur ###147852369$$$_RedirectToLoginPage_%%%963258741!!! A+ A A- हिन्दी | Sitemap Home People Recruitment Faculty Members Post Doctoral Fellows Technical Staff Members Project Staff Members Academic Programs Undergraduate Program Postgraduate Program Doctoral Program Curriculum Courses Program Structure Regulations Research Publication Research Groups Ongoing Projects Completed Projects Collaborations Laboratories Contact Physics Lata Panwar Lata Panwar Assistant Professor school PhD: Indian Institute of Science, Bangalore, Karnataka email lata[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Experimental High Energy Physics. call 0291 280 1625 language Web Profile Biography Dr. Lata Panwar is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Physics at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur. She joined the institute in April 2025. She earned her B.Sc. (Hons.) and M.Sc. degrees in Physics from the University of Rajasthan (2011 - 2014, 2014 - 2016), and completed her Ph.D. in Experimental High Energy Particle Physics at the Indian Institute of Science (IISc), Bangalore, in 2022. Her doctoral research, under the supervision of Dr. Jyothsna Rani Komaragiri, focused on searches for nonresonant and resonant Di-Higgs production at 13 TeV using proton-proton collision data from the CMS detector at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC), CERN. Following her Ph.D., Dr. Panwar pursued postdoctoral research at the Laboratoire de Physique Nucléaire et des Hautes Énergies (LPNHE)-CNRS-Sorbonne Université / Université Paris Cité, working with the ATLAS collaboration. She collaborated with Dr. Bogdan Malaescu, Dr. Luc Poggioli and Dr. Reina Camacho Toro on deriving in situ Jet Energy Scale (JES) calibrations for ATLAS and on Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) and Lund Jet Plane studies at ATLAS and at the proposed Future Circular Collider-electron-positron (FCC-ee) experiment. At IIT Jodhpur, Dr. Panwar is building a dynamic research group in Experimental High Energy Physics, focusing on Higgs and Jet Physics at the LHC and FCC. Research Our research group at IIT Jodhpur is a growing team engaged in cutting-edge research in the field of Experimental High Energy Physics (EHEP). We are actively involved in exploring fundamental aspects of particle physics through both current and future collider experiments. Our primary research interests include: Jet performance studies Data analyses using LHC datasets, with a focus on Higgs and QCD physics, including the application of modern techniques such as machine learning Projection and feasibility studies for the proposed Future Circular Collider (FCC) We invite enthusiastic students and researchers to collaborate with us and contribute to the growing landscape of experimental high energy physics. Indian Institute of Technology Delhi email amritapuri[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Active noise control; Active vibration control; Experimental modal analysis; Acoustics call 0291 280 1518 About Dr. Amrita Puri has been an assistant professor in Department of Mechanical Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur since July 2019. She completed her PhD in the field of active control of noise in vibro-acoustic cavities from Indian Institute of Technology, Delhi. Her PhD thesis work has been published in Mechanical Systems and Signal Processing, Journal of the Acoustical Society of America, Applied Acoustics, Journal of Sound and Vibration etc. She was awarded ‘Distinction in Doctoral Research for the year 2019’ by Indian Institute of Technology, Delhi. Prior to that, she did Master of Technology in Solid Mechanics and Design from Indian Institute of Technology, Kanpur. Her first PhD student is working in the field of spatial sound field synthesis techniques to render focused and non-focused moving sound sources. The work has been published in Journal of Audio Engineering Society. Currently, she is supervising 3 full time PhD students and 1 part time PhD student. She has taught undergraduate course of ‘Engineering Mechanics’ and postgraduate courses of ‘Introduction to Acoustics’, ‘Modeling and control of Mechanical systems’ and ‘Geometric modeling and CAD’. Currently, she is principal investigator of three sponsored research projects broadly in the field of sound control. Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee email monikadubey[at]iitj[dot]ac[dot]in biotech Water and wastewater treatment; Monitoring and removal of emerging contaminants; Bioremediation; Biotransformation of trace organic pollutants; Risk assessment for water reuse call 0291 280 1668 language Web Profile About: Dr. Monika Dubey is an Assistant Professor in the Department of Civil and Infrastructure Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jodhpur. Educational Background Dr. Dubey received her Ph.D. from the Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee, specializing in wastewater treatment, the fate of organic micropollutants, and environmental risk assessment. Research Interests Dr. Dubey’s research expertise lies in environmental monitoring, wastewater treatment, environmental remediation, and mass spectrometry techniques such as UHPLC-MS/MS, with a particular focus on emerging contaminants in the environment and their fate during wastewater treatment. She actively engages in collaborative and interdisciplinary research to develop innovative and sustainable solutions, contributing to advancements in sustainable wastewater management and environmental protection. Sustainable Environmental Systems (SES) Lab The Sustainable Environmental Systems (SES) Lab at IIT Jodhpur is dedicated to developing innovative and sustainable technologies for environmental protection and resource recovery. The research spans wastewater treatment, nature-based solutions, the fate and removal of emerging contaminants, bioelectrochemical processes, and carbon sequestration strategies. By integrating advanced analytical tools and AI-driven approaches, SES Lab aims to address critical challenges in water, environment, and climate sustainability. Research Positions Open Research positions are available in the fields of biological wastewater treatment, advanced oxidation processes for water and wastewater treatment, nature-based solutions, and micropollutant/transformation product analysis.
